 farhaan akhtar, arjuna rampal, purab kohli ke alaava film main shraddha kapur or shashaank arora najar aaenge

 tippaniyan 'rock On 2' will also feature Shraddha Kapoor and Shashank Arora (butterfly Fame) alongside Arjun Rampal, Farhan Akhtar and Poorab Kohli in lead roles
 is film se shujaat saudagar apane nirdesan kariyar kii shuruyaat kar rahe hai

 is film main shankar-ehsaan-loy mujeec denge or iske liye shraddha kapur ne bhi gane record kiye hai

 com / eop8w0rdhl khudara kshetra main pratyaksh videshi nivesh (epadiai) ke mudde par charchaa chaar-paanch disambar ko hogi or uske baad matdaan hoga
 The Congress-led United Progressive Alliance (UPA) government at the Center is confident of winning it
 sarkaar ne somvaar ko sabhi partiyon se apil kii ki ve is mudde par 'raajnneeti' se dur rahen
 Union Parliamentary Affairs Minister Kamal Nath told reporters, "we are confident about the number force
 " is mudde par sadan main charchaa ko 'puri tarah raajnneeti' qaraar dete hue unhone anya dalon se apil kii ki ve vipakshi dal bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) or marxvaadi communist party (makapa) kii ore se pryojit prastaav ko khaarij kar den
 Kamal Nath said, "I appeal to all parties to reject the politics of the motion and vote against politics in the House
" epadiai par centre kii niti spasht he ki rajyon ko ise lagu karne ke bare main nirnay lene kaa puraa adhikaar hoga
 " kamalnath ne yah bhi kaha ki yadi aavashyaktaa hui to sarkaar khudara kshetra main epadiai kii anumati dene ke liye aavashyak videshi vinimay prabandhan adhinium (femaa) main sanshodhan sansad ke donon sadanon se paarit karvaa legi
 He said, "according to the rules, it is enough to be passed by one house
 lekin yadi aavashyaktaa hoti he to ham ise donon sadanon main paarit karavaaenge
 " makapa netaa seetaram yechuri ne haal hi main kaha tha ki femaa sanshodhano kaa sansad ke donon sadanon se paarit hona aavashyak he
 If the government does not do so, it will be challenged in court
 bhaajapa bhi femaa sanshodhan vidheyak donon sadanon se paarit karaae jane kii maang kar rahi he
 Discussion is going on under Rule 184 in Lok Sabha and Rule 168 in Rajya Sabha
 donon niyamon main charchaa ke baad matdaan kaa praavdhaan he
 The central government is confident of having the numbers force in its favor in the lower house, while the number force in the upper house is not in its favor
 sutron kaa kahana he ki rajyasabha main epadiai par matdaan ko lekar samprag sarkaar ko baahar se samarthan de rahi samaajawaadee party (sapa) or bahujan samaaj party (basapa) kii bhoomika mahatvapurn hogi
 SP leader Ram Gopal Yadav has said last week that the party will oppose FDI in the Rajya Sabha
 lekin sarkari sutron ko bharosa he ki ve sapa ko manaane main kaamyaab honge
 The comments kendriya sansadeey kaary rajya mantri rajeev shukla ne kaha, "ham donon sadanon main samarthan ke liye anya dalon se baatcheet kar rahe hai
 " samprag kaa daawa he ki 245 sadasyeey rajyasabha main iske sadasyon kii sankhya 90 he, jabaki use baahar se samarthan dene vaali basapa, sapa tathaa lok janashakti party (lojpa) or rashtriya janata dal (rajd) ke saath iske paas 117 kaa sankhya bal he
 At the same time, the opposition claims that it has a strength of 110 members
 iske atirikt saat nirdaleey, choti partiyon ke paanch tathaa manonith sadasyon kii sankhya 10 he

 in dinon gujarat ke mukhyamantri narendra modi or unke dhur virdohi keshubhai patel ke bich kii jang khulkar saamne aa gai he or halaat bad se badtar hote ja rahe hai
 The battle took a worse turn on July 2 when 83-year-old Patel appealed to BJP workers to "overthrow those who believe in no repeat theory"
 unka ishaara khaas taur par modi kii sthaneey nikaay chunaavon main ummidavaaron ko na dohraane ke rujhaan kii ore tha
 Two days ago, former Gujarat Chief Minister Suresh Mehta indicated that they were considering setting up a third front under Patel's leadership
 mehta ke sanket ke baad 29 june ko patel samarthakon kii ek baithak hui jisamen sahmati jataai gai ki ek party ke rup main bijepi apana oj kho chuki he kyonki vah ''modi ke farmaanon ke aage puri tarah ghutane tech chuki he or unke khilaaf kuch bhi sunne kii icchhuk nahin he
 Patel will address eight public meetings in Ahmedabad, Vadodara, Surat and Rajkot under the banner of Parivartan Lok Jagriti Abhiyan
 in ilaakon main pradesh ke kul 182 vidhansabha kshetron main se 50 vidhansabha kshetra hai
 Mehta and Keshubhai plan to reduce Modi's strong base in urban areas as they believe Modi is weak in rural areas of the state
 unhen mahagujarat janata party ke gordhan jadfia kaa samarthan hasil he
 Assembly elections are due in Gujarat in December 2012
 patel kaa kahana he ki ve bijepi kii apni praathmik sadsyta kaa navinikaran nahin karavaaenge kyonki party ke saath unke sambandh khatm ho chuke hai
 He has turned his blog into a platform for malicious attacks against Modi
 june main unhone likhaa, ''yadi modi dilli chale jate hai to yah behatar hoga kyonki gujarat ko unke boj se chhutkaaraa mil jayega
 "in another attack, the former Chief Minister has written," BJP workers have turned into bonded laborers
 udyogpatiyon ke saath paanch sitara hotalon main baithkon ke dauraan unke saath achhuton jaisaa vyavhaar kiya jaataa he
 "so far, 61-year-old Modi has been avoiding reacting to Patel's provocative statements
" unhone yah bhi sunishchit kiya he ki gujarat bijepi netritv purv mukhyamantri ke jubaani hamalon kii upeksha kare
 The Chief Minister has his reasons for doing so
 pehla, unka maananaa he ki kisi tisare morche kii vajah se hone vaale maton ke bikharaav se unhen phayda pahunch saktaa he
 Second, he believes that his performance will testify on his own
